[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Fix Strategy[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<fix_strategy>[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. Root Cause Analysis[0m                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - The stack-buffer-overflow originates in dissect_ber_GeneralString [0m             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;39m([0m[39mpacket-ber.[0m[1;92mc:3194[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m. It reads the first content octet into an [0m[1;36m8[0m[39m-bit signed [0m         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`tvb_len`, then:[0m                                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     • If `tvb_len >= name_len`, copies `name_len-[0m[1;36m1[0m[39m` bytes into `name_string`.[0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     • Else copies `tvb_len` bytes.[0m                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     • Finally writes a NUL at `name_string[0m[1;39m[[0m[39mtvb_len[0m[1;39m][0m[39m`.[0m                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - When `tvb_len` [0m[1;39m([0m[39mpromoted to unsigned[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m is ≥ `name_len` [0m[1;39m([0m[1;36m80[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m, the code copies [0m[1;36m79[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mbytes but still writes at index `tvb_len ≥ [0m[1;36m80[0m[39m`, causing a one-byte overflow.[0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Furthermore, using `tvb_get_uint8` to determine string length is incorrect: [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mthe actual string length is the BER TLV length, not the first octet of its content.[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. High-Level Fix[0m                                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - In dissect_ber_GeneralString:[0m                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     a. Replace the ad-hoc `tvb_len = [0m[1;35mtvb_get_uint8[0m[1;39m([0m[33m...[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` logic with a robust [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mcomputation of the actual content length:[0m                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        ‑ Use [0m[1;35mtvb_reported_length_remaining[0m[1;39m([0m[39mout_tvb, [0m[1;36m0[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m to get the full byte length[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mof the GeneralString payload.[0m                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     b. Clamp the number of bytes copied to `name_len - [0m[1;36m1[0m[39m` to reserve space for the[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mterminating NUL.[0m                                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     c. Copy exactly `copy_len` bytes, then write the NUL at [0m                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`name_string[0m[1;39m[[0m[39mcopy_len[0m[1;39m][0m[39m`.[0m                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Remove the signed [0m[1;36m8[0m[39m-bit `tvb_len` entirely to avoid sign/unsigned conversion [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39missues.[0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Add a guard [0m[1;39m([0m[39massert or early return[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m if `name_len == [0m[1;36m0[0m[39m` to prevent unsigned [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39munderflow in pathological calls [0m[1;39m([0m[39mthough current callers always pass [0m                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;35msizeof[0m[1;39m([0m[39mbuffer[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m>[0m[1;36m0[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m.[0m                                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. Patch Implementation Steps[0m                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   [0m[1;36m1[0m[39m. Open epan/dissectors/packet-ber.c and locate function [0m                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mdissect_ber_GeneralString [0m[1;39m([0m[39maround line [0m[1;36m3174[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m.[0m                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   [0m[1;36m2[0m[39m. Change the local declarations:[0m                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      • Remove `int8_t tvb_len;`[0m                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      • Add `guint    content_len;` [0m[1;39m([0m[39mor `size_t content_len;`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m and `guint    [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mcopy_len;`.[0m                                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   [0m[1;36m3[0m[39m. After `if [0m[1;39m([0m[39mout_tvb[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m[39m … [0m[1;39m}[0m[39m`, replace lines [0m[1;36m3188[0m[39m–[0m[1;36m3194[0m[39m with:[0m                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      ```[0m                                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        [0m[35m/[0m[39m* Determine actual payload length and clamp to buffer size - [0m[1;36m1[0m[39m *[0m[35m/[0m          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        content_len = [0m[1;35mtvb_reported_length_remaining[0m[1;39m([0m[39mout_tvb, [0m[1;36m0[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        if [0m[1;39m([0m[39mname_len == [0m[1;36m0[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m            [0m[35m/[0m[39m* Defensive: no space for string *[0m[35m/[0m                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m            return offset;[0m                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        copy_len = [0m[1;39m([0m[39mcontent_len >= name_len[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m ? [0m[1;39m([0m[39mname_len - [0m[1;36m1[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m : content_len;[0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        [0m[1;35mtvb_memcpy[0m[1;39m([0m[39mout_tvb, [0m[1;39m([0m[39mguint8 *[0m[1;39m)[0m[39mname_string, [0m[1;36m0[0m[39m, copy_len[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        name_string[0m[1;39m[[0m[39mcopy_len[0m[1;39m][0m[39m = [0m[32m'\0'[0m[39m;[0m                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      ```[0m                                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   [0m[1;36m4[0m[39m. Remove any remaining references to `tvb_len`.[0m                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   [0m[1;36m5[0m[39m. Build and run AddressSanitizer-instrumented tests to confirm the overflow is [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39meliminated.[0m                                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   [0m[1;36m6[0m[39m. Run the existing fuzzing harness to verify no regression is introduced.[0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m4[0m[39m. Preservation of Functionality[0m                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - We still extract and NUL-terminate GeneralString content; only the length [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39msource and bounds checks are corrected.[0m                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - The clamped copy ensures no overflow, but strings longer than `name_len-[0m[1;36m1[0m[39m` are[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mtruncated—matching typical C string safety practices.[0m                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - All other BER dissector logic remains untouched.[0m                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m5[0m[39m. Side Effects & Mitigations[0m                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Truncation: very long GeneralString values are truncated to [0m[1;36m79[0m[39m bytes—unlikely [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mto break display or protocol analysis, acceptable for a UI buffer.[0m                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - No impact on other string types or the fuzzer harness.[0m                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Ensure `name_len` passed by callers remains accurate [0m[1;39m([0m[39msizeof buffer[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m; if [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mfuture callers pass custom buffers, they must also observe the >[0m[1;36m0[0m[39m requirement.[0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m6[0m[39m. References[0m                                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Similar safe-copy patterns in other Wireshark string dissectors [0m[1;39m([0m[39me.g., [0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mUTF8String handlers use explicit length checks[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m.[0m                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Aligns with existing codebase practice: always reserve one byte for `[0m[32m'\0'[0m[39m` [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mwhen copying into fixed buffers.[0m                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mfix_strategy[0m[1m>[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         ===Evaluation [33mEnd[0m===                                                                [2m                [0m
